# A

[Back to index](index.md)

## aabalat

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `AABALAT`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to ablate components, remove parts for testing, or measure contribution by absence
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** technology-software, ai-cognition, media-communication
- **Root family:** `ABLT`; Technology; ablation, component-removal test; ablation, removal test, learning what a component contributes by taking it away
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** A-B-L-T root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na aabalat.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

## aabalat-da

- **Part of speech:** particle
- **Definition:** open; unhidden
- **Register/status:** grammar; accepted

- **Example:** Leb en na e ap kot.

### Sense 3: particle

- **Pronunciation:** `AP`
- **Part of speech:** particle:aspect
- **Definition:** open; unhidden
- **Register/status:** aspect; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** Marks disclosed or unguarded state.
- **Example:** Leb en na e ap kot.
- **Corpus:** common (240 attestations); tracks: civic-law, daily-dialogues, learner-graded, literary-poetic, ritual-vow, technical-software; examples in civic-015, civic-054, civic-062, civic-068, civic-093, civic-098, daily-050, daily-064, ...
